### Quantum Physics

### Wave Mechanics

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[u_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = U_{\mathrm{P_1}}u_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \qquad U_{\mathrm{P_1}} = T_{\mathrm{wave}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{wave}}, \qquad \|U_{\mathrm{P_1}}\| \le 1\]

  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.
  Reading: fluid carriage / root fixation / structural fixation line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: fluid carriage / root fixation / structural fixation line.
  Confidence: mixed
